                  .then(function(response) {
                      return response.json();
                  })
                  .then(function(data) {
                      FLAGS[flagName] = data.is_active;
                      if (data.is_active_experiment) {
                          EXPERIMENTS[flagName] = {
                              gaExperimentId: data.ga_experiment_id,
                              chosenVariation: data.is_active ? '1' : '0',
                          };
                          waffle.sendGAExperiment(flagName);
                      }
                      return data.is_active
                  })
                  .catch(function (data) {
                      return false;
                  });
        },
        sendGAExperiment: function (flagName) {
            var expData = EXPERIMENTS[flagName];
            if (!expData) {
                return;
            }

            if (expData.chosenVariation === '1') {
                window.hj = window.hj||function(){(hj.q=hj.q||[]).push(arguments)};
                window.hj('trigger', flagName);
                window.hj('tagRecording', [flagName]);
            }

            var variant = expData.chosenVariation === '0' ? 'A' : 'B';
            window.dataLayer = window.dataLayer || [];
            try {
                window.dataLayer.push({
                    event: 'Personal_Account',
                    eventCategory: 'A/B Test DataLayer',
                    eventAction: flagName,
                    eventLabel: 'Variant ' + variant,
                });
                var opts = {
                    nonInteraction: true
                };
                if (expData.gaExperimentId) {
                      {
                          opts.expId = expData.gaExperimentId;
                          opts.expVar = expData.chosenVariation;
                      }
                }
                ga('send', 'event', 'A/B Test', flagName, 'Variant ' + variant, opts);
                recordExperimentLog(flagName, variant, expData);
            } catch (e) {
                // do nothing
                window.dataLayer.push({
                    event: 'Personal_Account',
                    eventCategory: 'A/B Test DataLayer',
                    eventAction: 'ERROR',
                    eventLabel: e,
                });
            }
        },
        sendGAExperimentsOnPageLoad: function () {
            for (var flagName in EXPERIMENTS) {
                var expData = EXPERIMENTS[flagName];
                if (expData.sendFromJS === true) {
                    continue;
                }
                waffle.sendGAExperiment(flagName);
            }
        },
        switch_is_active: function waffle_switch(switch_name) {
            return !!SWITCHES[switch_name];
        },
    };
})();

        (function() {
    var ANNOUNCEMENTS = JSON.parse('[{\u0022priority\u0022: 100, \u0022text\u0022: \u0022\u003Cspan class\u003D\u005C\u0022m\u005C\u0022\u003E\u005Cn            Today only!\u005Cn            \u003C/span\u003E\u005Cn            Book a lesson with any tutor and receive 50%\u005Cn            off this lesson at checkout! Book today, learn any day.\u005Cn        \u003Cspan class\u003D\u005C\u0022text\u002Dfaded\u005C\u0022\u003EFirst time offer\u003C/span\u003E\u0022, \u0022title\u0022: \u0022Discount 50\u0022}]');

    window.yell = {
        ANNOUNCEMENTS: ANNOUNCEMENTS,

        getFirstActive: function() {
            if (_.isEmpty(ANNOUNCEMENTS)) {
                return;
            }
            return ANNOUNCEMENTS.filter(function(ann) {
                return !(ann.active === false);
            }).sort(function(a, b) {
                return b.priority - a.priority;
            })[0];
    },
};
})();
  </script>

     Ocultar
    </a>
   </div>
   <script>
    var getCookieNew =  function(cname){
                                    var name = cname + "=";
                                    var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
                                    for(var i=0; i<ca.length; i++) {
                                        var c = ca[i].trim();
                                        if (c.indexOf(name)==0) return c.substring(name.length,c.length);
                                    }
                                    return "";
                                }
            var setCookieNew = function(cname, cvalue, exdays){
                                    var d = new Date();
                                    exdays = exdays || 365;
                                    d.setTime(d.getTime()+(exdays * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000));
                                    var expires = "expires="+d.toGMTString();
                                    document.cookie = cname + "=" + cvalue + "; " + expires + ";path=/"
            }
            var cookieConsent = document.getElementById("eu_cookies_block");

            if(getCookieNew('eu_cookie_policy') != 'yes')
            {
                cookieConsent.setAttribute("style", "z-index: 99;" +
                    "position:fixed;left:0;right:0;bottom:0;padding: 10px 0 4px 0;background: #333;text-align: center;font-size: 12px;color: #ccc !important;")
            }else{
                 cookieConsent.setAttribute("style", "display:none;z-index: 99;!important;position: fixed;left: 0;right: 0;bottom: 0;padding: 10px 0 4px 0;background: #333;text-align: center;font-size: 12px;color: #ccc !important;")

            }
            cookieConsent.onclick = function(){
                setCookieNew('eu_cookie_policy', 'yes');
                cookieConsent.setAttribute("style", "display:none;");
            }
   </script>
   <script>
    window.addEventListener('load', function () {
        (function (d, s, id) {
            var js, fjs = d.getElementsByTagName(s)[0];
            if (d.getElementById(id)) return;
            js = d.createElement(s);
            js.id = id;
            js.src = "//connect.facebook.net/en_US/all.js#xfbml=1&appId=414960338557731";
            fjs.parentNode.insertBefore(js, fjs);
        }(document, 'script', 'facebook-jssdk'));

        window.___gcfg = {
            lang: 'en-US',
            parsetags: 'explicit'
        };

        (function () {
            var po = document.createElement('script');
            po.type = 'text/javascript';
            po.async = true;
            po.src = 'https://apis.google.com/js/plusone.js';
            var s = document.getElementsByTagName('script')[0];
            s.parentNode.insertBefore(po, s);
        })();
    });

   <script>
    function getStrTimeShift(minutes){
        var date = new Date();
        date.setTime(date.getTime() + (minutes*60*1000));
        return date.toUTCString();
    }

    (function (globals) {

  var django = globals.django || (globals.django = {});


  django.pluralidx = function (n) {
    var v=(n==1 ? 0 : n%10>=2 && n%10<=4 && (n%100<10 || n%100>=20) ? 1 : 2);
    if (typeof(v) == 'boolean') {
      return v ? 1 : 0;
    } else {
      return v;
    }
  };

  django.gettext = function (msgid) {
    var value = django.catalog[msgid];
    if (typeof(value) == 'undefined') {
      return msgid;
    } else {
      return (typeof(value) == 'string') ? value : value[0];
    }
  };

  django.ngettext = function (singular, plural, count) {
    var value = django.catalog[singular];
    if (typeof(value) == 'undefined') {
      return (count == 1) ? singular : plural;
    } else {
      return value[django.pluralidx(count)];
    }
  };

  django.gettext_noop = function (msgid) { return msgid; };

  django.pgettext = function (context, msgid) {
    var value = django.gettext(context + '\x04' + msgid);
    if (value.indexOf('\x04') != -1) {
      value = msgid;
    }
    return value;
  };

  django.npgettext = function (context, singular, plural, count) {
    var value = django.ngettext(context + '\x04' + singular, context + '\x04' + plural, count);
    if (value.indexOf('\x04') != -1) {
      value = django.ngettext(singular, plural, count);
    }
    return value;
  };


  django.interpolate = function (fmt, obj, named) {
    if (named) {
      return fmt.replace(/%\(\w+\)s/g, function(match){return String(obj[match.slice(2,-2)])});
    } else {
      return fmt.replace(/%s/g, function(match){return String(obj.shift())});
    }
  };


  /* formatting library */

  django.formats = {
    "DATETIME_FORMAT": "N j, Y, P",
    "DATETIME_INPUT_FORMATS": [
      "%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S",
      "%Y-%m-%d %H:%M",
      "%Y-%m-%d",
      "%m/%d/%Y %H:%M:%S",
      "%m/%d/%Y %H:%M",
      "%m/%d/%Y",
      "%m/%d/%y %H:%M:%S",
      "%m/%d/%y %H:%M",
      "%m/%d/%y"
    ],
    "DATE_FORMAT": "N j, Y",
    "DATE_INPUT_FORMATS": [
      "%Y-%m-%d",
      "%m/%d/%Y",
      "%m/%d/%y"
    ],
    "DECIMAL_SEPARATOR": ".",
    "FIRST_DAY_OF_WEEK": "0",
    "MONTH_DAY_FORMAT": "F j",
    "NUMBER_GROUPING": "3",
    "SHORT_DATETIME_FORMAT": "m/d/Y P",
    "SHORT_DATE_FORMAT": "m/d/Y",
    "THOUSAND_SEPARATOR": ",",
    "TIME_FORMAT": "P",
    "TIME_INPUT_FORMATS": [
      "%H:%M:%S",
      "%H:%M"
    ],
    "YEAR_MONTH_FORMAT": "F Y"
  };

  django.get_format = function (format_type) {
    var value = django.formats[format_type];
    if (typeof(value) == 'undefined') {
      return format_type;
    } else {
      return value;
    }
  };

  /* add to global namespace */
  globals.pluralidx = django.pluralidx;
  globals.gettext = django.gettext;
  globals.ngettext = django.ngettext;
  globals.gettext_noop = django.gettext_noop;
  globals.pgettext = django.pgettext;
  globals.npgettext = django.npgettext;
  globals.interpolate = django.interpolate;
  globals.get_format = django.get_format;

}(this));
   </script>
